test_help_flag_works_with_env_system (tests.integration.test_env_integration.TestEnvironmentIntegration)
Test that help flag works even with new environment system. ... usage: artist_bio_gen [-h] --input-file INPUT_FILE [--version VERSION]
                      [--output OUTPUT] [--max-workers MAX_WORKERS]
                      [--dry-run] [--verbose] [--enable-db] [--test-mode]
                      [--resume] [--openai-api-key OPENAI_API_KEY]
                      [--prompt-id PROMPT_ID] [--db-url DB_URL]
                      [--quota-monitoring {true,false}]
                      [--quota-threshold QUOTA_THRESHOLD]
                      [--daily-limit DAILY_LIMIT]
                      [--pause-duration PAUSE_DURATION]
                      [--quota-log-interval QUOTA_LOG_INTERVAL]

Generate artist bios using OpenAI Responses API

optional arguments:
  -h, --help            show this help message and exit
  --input-file INPUT_FILE
                        CSV-like text file path containing artist data
  --version VERSION     Prompt version (optional)
  --output OUTPUT       JSONL output file path (default: out.jsonl)
  --max-workers MAX_WORKERS
                        Maximum number of concurrent requests (default: 4)
  --dry-run             Parse inputs and show first 5 payloads without making
                        API calls
  --verbose             Enable verbose logging (DEBUG level)
  --enable-db           Enable database updates (requires DATABASE_URL env
                        var)
  --test-mode           Use test_artists table instead of artists table
  --resume              Resume processing by skipping artists already present
                        in output file
  --openai-api-key OPENAI_API_KEY
                        OpenAI API key for authentication
  --prompt-id PROMPT_ID
                        OpenAI prompt ID
  --db-url DB_URL       Database connection URL
  --quota-monitoring {true,false}
                        Enable or disable quota monitoring
  --quota-threshold QUOTA_THRESHOLD
                        Pause threshold as a decimal between 0.1 and 1.0
  --daily-limit DAILY_LIMIT
                        Optional daily request limit used for pausing
  --pause-duration PAUSE_DURATION
                        Hours to pause when quota is hit (1-72)
  --quota-log-interval QUOTA_LOG_INTERVAL
                        Log quota metrics every N requests to reduce noise

Examples: python run_artists.py --input-file artists.csv --prompt-id
prompt_123 python run_artists.py --input-file data.txt --max-workers 8 python
run_artists.py --input-file artists.csv --dry-run
ok
